%%\tagged{Ans@ShortAns, Type@Compute, Topic@Integral, Sub@Improper, Func@Exp, File@0072}{
\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0072. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{2}^{\infty}{{\frac{e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 8}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{2}^{\infty}{{\frac{e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 8}}\;dx} = \answer{-\frac{1}{8} \, \sqrt{2} \log\left(\frac{e^{4} - 8}{4 \, \sqrt{2} e^{2} + e^{4} + 8}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0072. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{4}^{\infty}{{-\frac{3 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 5}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{4}^{\infty}{{-\frac{3 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 5}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{3}{10} \, \sqrt{5} \log\left(\frac{e^{8} - 5}{2 \, \sqrt{5} e^{4} + e^{8} + 5}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0072. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

\int_{-8}^{\infty}{{-\frac{7 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 3}}\;dx}

\choice{Diverges}

\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}

\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0072. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{-1}^{\infty}{{-\frac{4 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 1}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{-1}^{\infty}{{-\frac{4 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 1}}\;dx} = \answer{-2 \, \log\left({\left(e + 1\right)} e^{\left(-1\right)}\right) + 2 \, \log\left(-{\left(e - 1\right)} e^{\left(-1\right)}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\int_{3}^{\infty}{{-\frac{e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 5}}\;dx} = \answer{-\frac{1}{10} \, \sqrt{5} \pi + \frac{1}{5} \, \sqrt{5} \arctan\left(\frac{1}{5} \, \sqrt{5} e^{3}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\int_{-3}^{\infty}{{-\frac{3 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 8}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{-3}^{\infty}{{-\frac{3 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 8}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{3}{8} \, \sqrt{2} \log\left(-\frac{8 \, e^{6} - 1}{4 \, \sqrt{2} e^{3} + 8 \, e^{6} + 1}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0072. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{-7}^{\infty}{{-\frac{6 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 7}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{-7}^{\infty}{{-\frac{6 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 7}}\;dx} = \answer{-\frac{3}{7} \, \sqrt{7} \pi + \frac{6}{7} \, \sqrt{7} \arctan\left(\frac{1}{7} \, \sqrt{7} e^{\left(-7\right)}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\end{multipleChoice}

\end{problem}

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{5}^{\infty}{{-\frac{5 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 1}}\;dx} = \answer{-\frac{5}{2} \, \log\left(e^{5} + 1\right) + \frac{5}{2} \, \log\left(e^{5} - 1\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\int_{4}^{\infty}{{\frac{4 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 2}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{4}^{\infty}{{\frac{4 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 2}}\;dx} = \answer{\sqrt{2} \pi - 2 \, \sqrt{2} \arctan\left(\frac{1}{2} \, \sqrt{2} e^{4}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0072. \\ \fi

\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{-3}^{\infty}{{-\frac{e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 4}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{-3}^{\infty}{{-\frac{e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 4}}\;dx} = \answer{-\frac{1}{4} \, \log\left({\left(2 \, e^{3} + 1\right)} e^{\left(-3\right)}\right) + \frac{1}{4} \, \log\left(-{\left(2 \, e^{3} - 1\right)} e^{\left(-3\right)}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{7}^{\infty}{{-\frac{8 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 1}}\;dx} = \answer{-4 \, \pi + 8 \, \arctan\left(e^{7}\right)}

\end{problem}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0072. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{2}^{\infty}{{-\frac{8 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 2}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{2}^{\infty}{{-\frac{8 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 2}}\;dx} = \answer{-2 \, \sqrt{2} \pi + 4 \, \sqrt{2} \arctan\left(\frac{1}{2} \, \sqrt{2} e^{2}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0072. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{3}^{\infty}{{-\frac{8 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 3}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{3}^{\infty}{{-\frac{8 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 3}}\;dx} = \answer{-\frac{4}{3} \, \sqrt{3} \pi + \frac{8}{3} \, \sqrt{3} \arctan\left(\frac{1}{3} \, \sqrt{3} e^{3}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0072. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{3}^{\infty}{{-\frac{6 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 6}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{3}^{\infty}{{-\frac{6 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 6}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{1}{2} \, \sqrt{6} \log\left(\frac{e^{6} - 6}{2 \, \sqrt{6} e^{3} + e^{6} + 6}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0072. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{-6}^{\infty}{{\frac{3 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 9}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{-6}^{\infty}{{\frac{3 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 9}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{1}{2} \, \log\left({\left(3 \, e^{6} + 1\right)} e^{\left(-6\right)}\right) - \frac{1}{2} \, \log\left(-{\left(3 \, e^{6} - 1\right)} e^{\left(-6\right)}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\]

\end{problem}

\[
\int_{5}^{\infty}{{-\frac{5 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 3}}\;dx}

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{5}^{\infty}{{-\frac{5 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 3}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{5}{6} \, \sqrt{3} \log\left(\frac{e^{10} - 3}{2 \, \sqrt{3} e^{5} + e^{10} + 3}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\int_{4}^{\infty}{{\frac{3 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 8}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{4}^{\infty}{{\frac{3 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 8}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{3}{8} \, \sqrt{2} \pi - \frac{3}{4} \, \sqrt{2} \arctan\left(\frac{1}{4} \, \sqrt{2} e^{4}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0072. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{1}^{\infty}{{\frac{e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 3}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{1}^{\infty}{{\frac{e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 3}}\;dx} = \answer{-\frac{1}{6} \, \sqrt{3} \log\left(\frac{e^{2} - 3}{2 \, \sqrt{3} e + e^{2} + 3}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\end{problem}

\int_{3}^{\infty}{{-\frac{8 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} - 1}}\;dx} = \answer{-4 \, \log\left(e^{3} + 1\right) + 4 \, \log\left(e^{3} - 1\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\int_{2}^{\infty}{{\frac{2 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 7}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0072.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{2}^{\infty}{{\frac{2 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 7}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{1}{7} \, \sqrt{7} \pi - \frac{2}{7} \, \sqrt{7} \arctan\left(\frac{1}{7} \, \sqrt{7} e^{2}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\[
\int_{4}^{\infty}{{\frac{2 \, e^{x}}{e^{\left(2 \, x\right)} + 9}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{1}{3} \, \pi - \frac{2}{3} \, \arctan\left(\frac{1}{3} \, e^{4}\right)}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\[

\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\]

\end{problem}
